For each of the original names, this files finds
the most similiar counterpart in the new names dataset using the LCS algorithm,
a sequence similarity algorithm, and
finding any new names such that the new name is a subset of the original name or
the original name is a subset of the new name.Original Name: New Name (LCS), New Name (Sequence Similarity), [Subset Names]
